These two points have been roughly agreed upon. However, the details are still unknown to the outside world. The future defense and salary distribution of foreign troops in Shanxi, such as Song Zheyuan's troops, are still to be discussed separately. Song and Pang Bingxun have now arrived in Tianjin, and Sun Dianying will also arrive tomorrow or the day after. Generally, it is not difficult to reach a satisfactory solution. According to Pang Bingxun, Feng's troops currently have about 60,000 people, including Sun Liangcheng's troops of more than 20,000, Song's troops of less than 20,000, Pang's troops of more than 10,000, and Gao Guizi's troops of 6,000-7,000. The most urgent problem to be solved for these 60,000 people is the issue of military pay. If there is a solution to the supply problem, it will be very easy to reorganize and mobilize them. (December 17th)

Establishment of Three Suppression Committees in Jiangxi Province 72

Luo and Zhang Have Assumed the Positions of Chairman and Committee Member

Headquarters of the Generalissimo Issues Suppression Regulations

Nanchang Telegram: When Chairman Jiang was in Nanchang, he decided to divide the southwestern region of Jiangxi Province, where banditry was most rampant, into three major bandit suppression and village cleansing areas. Each area would form a suppression committee. Currently, the three suppression committees of Ji'an, Yongfeng, and Le'an have been established one after another. Wei Lin, Zhang Huizan, and Tan Daoyuan have respectively assumed the positions of chairman and committee member and are actively suppressing bandits in accordance with the plan issued by the Generalissimo's Headquarters. The regulations issued by the Generalissimo's Headquarters are recorded below: (1) In order to achieve effective cooperation between the party, government, and military and fundamentally eliminate banditry, suppression committees and village cleansing committees should be established in the bandit suppression areas of Jiangxi Province, which will be guided separately by the Generalissimo's Headquarters and the Jiangxi Provincial Government. (2) In order to concentrate the existing talent and economic resources on eliminating the main force of the communist bandits in Donggu and Shaxi, suppression committees and village cleansing committees should be established in Ji'an, Yongfeng, and Le'an counties. (3) The county governments and county party headquarters in the areas where suppression committees and village cleansing committees are established should accept the command of the committees. (4) Each village cleansing and bandit suppression committee may include nearby counties within its management scope. The scope of the three committees of Le'an, Yongfeng, and Ji'an is temporarily set as follows: (A) Le'an District includes Yihuang, Chongren, Linchuan, Nanfeng, and Guangchang counties. (B) Yongfeng District includes Xiajiang, Xingan, Qingjiang, and Fengcheng counties. (C) Ji'an District includes Jishui, Taihe, and Anfu counties. (5) The village cleansing and bandit suppression committee is composed of the division commander stationed in the area, the chief of staff, the committee member sent to the area by the provincial party headquarters, the captain of the propaganda team sent by the Generalissimo's Headquarters, the county magistrate, and the county party committee member. (6) The division commander serves as the chairman of the committee. (7) The village cleansing and bandit suppression committee meets at least every other day to study the reports collected daily from the military, county government, and county party headquarters, criticize the appropriateness of their actions, guide them to correct their mistakes, effectively direct their activities, and send personnel to conduct practical inspections at any time. (8) The village cleansing and bandit suppression committee should fully guide and assist the county magistrate in carrying out household registration and baojia militia training. (9) If it is necessary to add or expand the management area of the suppression committee, the Generalissimo's Headquarters or the Jiangxi Provincial Government will decide at any time. (December 19th)

Panic Among Merchants and Farmers in Jilin Province 73

Chamber of Commerce Calls for Relief Measures

Provincial Order to Banks and Businesses to Provide Loans for Maintenance

Jilin Telegram: The industrial and commercial sectors of this province were previously affected by the Jin Gui incident,

Resulting in Extreme Financial Difficulties. The Provincial General Chamber of Commerce and the General Chamber of Industry jointly petitioned the provincial authorities to instruct various Banks and Businesses to provide loans for assistance. The Bureau of Finance convened a meeting of leaders from the industrial and commercial sectors and decided that the chamber would investigate the required amount and negotiate with various Banks and Businesses. It was expected that the autumn harvest would be approaching, and the market would be active, so the matter was delayed. However, although the harvest was abundant, the only special product that was relied upon to absorb cash and facilitate turnover was very sluggish in sales and showed no signs of loosening. The grain price continued to fall. The reasons were that the needs of various places were greatly reduced due to the abundant harvest, and the general economic relations and transport merchants were suspended. Even the Japanese merchants, who had always been major customers, increased their hesitations and stopped moving forward. In addition to industry and commerce, the farmers were also suffering from low grain prices. Everyone was complaining. Now that the end of the year is approaching, the merchants are in urgent need of money. The General Chamber of Commerce could not bear to sit idly by, so they re-proposed the old matter and requested the issuance of more Harbin currency and ordered various Banks and Businesses to fully lend to relieve the plight. At the end of last month, Chen You presented a petition to the Provincial Government through the Jilin Provincial Chamber of Commerce, calling for prompt approval. The original text roughly stated that (at present, the fields are full of harvested grain and grain carts are gathering. According to the historical situation in Jilin, the prices of various round coins should gradually decrease. However, all Banks and Businesses in Harbin have stopped lending. The financial situation in various commercial ports inside and outside the province is also tight, making it difficult to make ends meet. This has led to the decline of all industries and the increase in the price of money. All these states are not a blessing for the local area. Therefore, we sincerely request the relevant authorities to allow extra support.

Increase the amount of Harbin currency and order all official and commercial Banks and Businesses in various ports to fully understand the situation and fully lend to provide relief and facilitate circulation), etc. After receiving the report, the Provincial Government believed that the difficulty in turnover due to the scarcity of Harbin currency for transactions between various commercial firms inside and outside the province was indeed real. However, increasing the amount of Harbin currency without a reason would destroy the established plan, and it would be difficult to guarantee that the money dealers who control the market for profit would not stir up a financial panic and cause a crisis. Therefore, the first step of the request cannot be approved. However, since various places are in distress, the market is sluggish, the price of money continues to rise, and the grain merchants have no way to retreat, and the commercial and agricultural sectors are at a loss, we must also urgently seek relief. It is appropriate to instruct the official and commercial Banks and Businesses to understand the situation so as to facilitate circulation. Yesterday, the competent authorities have been ordered to forward the order to various Banks and Businesses and directly order the Yongheng Official Bank to comply with the order. At the same time, a consultation will be sent to the Harbin Special Region Commissioner's Office to forward the order to various Banks and Businesses in Harbin to provide sufficient loans to alleviate the urgent need. How to implement it is still under negotiation.

Liaoning Provincial Government Formulates Regulations for Financial Management 74

Standardize Finance and Prohibit the Exit of Silver Dollars

Shenyang Telegram: Since the Bianye Bank of Liaoning Province, the Official Bank of the Three Eastern Provinces, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications jointly established a four-bank reserve in the winter of last year, issuing Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates to circulate in the market, the Liaoning Provincial Government has formulated the Liaoning Provincial Regulations for Financial Management and the Regulations for Prohibiting the Exit of Cash in order to manage the four-bank reserve and reorganize the financial situation of the province. The regulations were submitted to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for promulgation and implementation. The regulations at that time were mainly established for the reserve, and their provisions referred to the Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates issued by the reserve. This year, the local financial situation is extremely tight. The General Office of the Official Bank of the Three Eastern Provinces submitted a report to the Provincial Government to issue 10 million yuan of Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates in response to market needs, which were issued in two phases. The first phase was 5 million yuan, and it was planned to issue more depending on the need. The content of the previous regulations for financial management was still not comprehensive enough, and the financial situation this year was different from previous years, so it was urgent to revise them to be observed together. The Provincial Government has separately revised the name to the Liaoning Provincial Regulations for Financial Management. The full text of the eleven articles, which were discussed, amended, and passed at the Provincial Government Committee meeting on the 16th of this month, is copied below: (Article 1) In order to standardize finance and prohibit the exit of Silver Dollars, the Liaoning Provincial Provisional Regulations for Financial Management are specifically established. (Article 2) The financial standard in this province is the Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates issued by the Official Bank and the Four-Bank Reserve (hereinafter referred to as the Reserve). (Article 3) After the Official Bank and the Reserve issue Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates in this province, the cash banknotes issued by other banks in foreign ports should be gradually recovered immediately, but the Silver Dollar Certificates of the Bianye Bank that have been approved on a special case basis are not included in this restriction. (Article 4) The Provincial Government will supervise the cash reserve of the Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates issued by the Official Bank and the Reserve at any time. (Article 5) The Silver Dollar Certificates issued by the Official Bank and the Reserve and the Silver Dollars are generally used and must not be discounted. Those who violate this will be severely punished. (Article 6) The Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates issued by the Official Bank and the Reserve can be exchanged for Silver Dollars or Silver Dollar banknotes of the same standard at the exchange offices in the provincial capital. (Article 7) The Silver Dollar Exchange Certificates issued by the Official Bank and the Reserve are permitted to be remitted by merchants and civilians without limitation, and remittance fees may be charged according to the market situation. (Article 8) In order to stabilize the financial situation in this province, it is prohibited to transport Silver Dollars out of the provincial capital. The aforementioned scope of the provincial capital refers to the area under the jurisdiction of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, that is, the urban area of Shenyang and the commercial port bureau. Going beyond this area is considered leaving the area. (Article 9) Military and police agencies will send people to guard and inspect each customs checkpoint, railway station, and wharf. If anyone is found carrying cash out of the area, the military and police will confiscate the Silver Dollars and turn them over to the government, and impose a penalty for the crime of disrupting the financial situation. A portion of the confiscated funds will be used as a reward, but carrying Silver Dollars less than 100 yuan is permitted and is not restricted. (Article 10) These regulations may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered. (Article 11) These regulations will be implemented from the date of promulgation. (December 17th)

Suggestions from Wuhu Business Community on Abolishing Li Taxes 75

Advocating that Rice Should be Exempt from Taxes

And Requesting Strict Abolition of Regular Customs

Wuhu Telegram: The Ministry of Finance has issued a nationwide telegram deciding to abolish Li Taxes on January 1, 2020. However, it is necessary to carefully plan for the compensation methods after the abolition of Li Taxes. The Ministry of Finance has specially sent commissioners to various provinces to solicit opinions from merchants and civilians. The special commissioner sent to Anhui Province was Zuo Xingjin. After Mr. Zuo came to Wuhu, the General Chamber of Commerce held several meetings to study this matter. Recently, a letter of recommendation has been drafted to respond to the special commissioner and request that it be forwarded to the Ministry of Finance. The original text is as follows (This time, your committee was ordered to come to Wuhu to investigate the production and sales of special goods and the Li Taxes borne. We accepted the six questions and the investigation form, and we saw the Ministry of Finance's intention to reduce the burden on merchants and accept the opinions of merchants. As for the first question, what are the important bulk products of Anhui Province besides rice? Most of the rice is transported by steamship to Guangdong and Chaozhou, and by sailboat to Jiangsu Province. Taxes are heavy and there are many items. The party and the government attach importance to people's livelihood, and rice should be exempt from taxes. After this abolition of Li Taxes, all rice and wheat transported shall no longer be subject to taxes. This is the first request of the merchants. As for the second and third questions, tea, wood, silk, paper, oil, and porcelain are all from Liuan and Huizhou. Tea Li Taxes are collected by special offices, and cocoon donations are also collected on the spot by special commissioners. They are currently handled by the Anhui Financial and Political Special Envoy Office. The rest, such as wood, paper, oil, and porcelain, all come from the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. Silk comes from Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The total number and name of taxes paid in Anhui Province can be found in the files of the Special Envoy Office and the New Regular Customs. If the above six items are changed to special taxes, they should be collected at the origin and export of the six items of goods. No new tax items should be added in Anhui Province. This is the second request of the merchants. As for the fifth question, what is the best method to compensate after the abolition of Li Taxes? The sixth question asks what is the pain of Li Taxes felt by merchants and how should other taxes be changed to satisfy the wishes of merchants? The abolition of Li Taxes refers to all taxes with the nature of transit taxes, similar to Li Taxes. According to the decision of the Abolition of Li Taxes Meeting in the 18th year, the following should be abolished in addition to Li Taxes: 1. Railway freight donations, 2. Parcel post taxes, 3. Regular taxes and surcharges within 50 miles of commercial ports, 4. Sub-port taxes and surcharges of maritime and land new customs, 5. Re-import taxes and surcharges of maritime and land new customs, 6. Export taxes and surcharges of maritime and land new customs from this port to that port, 7. Regular customs and surcharges within 50 miles of commercial ports. The implementation of the abolition of Li Taxes this time is to complete the unfinished work of the previous Abolition of Li Taxes Meeting. All the original resolutions were based on the requests of the business community and were determined after careful consideration. Now, they should still be the same and all seven items should be abolished in stages. However, the pain of regular customs felt by merchants is no less than that of Li Taxes. Chinese contractors will embezzle profits, and foreign contractors will exploit profits. The inspection is everywhere (the regular customs inspectors wear red belts, and merchants call them red belts). They are like wolves and tigers, and they impose fines on the road for every grain of rice and every chicken. If the customs system is not eliminated, the pain will not end. The regular customs should be abolished at the same time on January 1 next year to eliminate the pain of merchants. This is the third request of the merchants. As for the compensation issue, the Abolition of Li Taxes Meeting divided the items into business tax and special consumption tax. After careful consideration of the advantages and disadvantages, business tax is not as simple and easy to implement as special consumption tax. However, it must be implemented in accordance with the four principles of the Special Consumption Tax Implementation Outline of the previous resolution: (1) One tax for one item, such as returning the cocoon tax after paying the silk tax. (2) After one tax, it is applicable nationwide. (3) The tax amount of the consumption tax changed from the abolition of Li Taxes shall not be higher than the original tax amount. (4) It must be a bulk product within the jurisdiction, otherwise no tax shall be collected. If these four principles can be strictly adhered to, the tax rate will not be changed and the burden will not be increased. This is the fourth request of the merchants. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce suggests that because Jiangxi and Fujian provinces have implemented special consumption taxes, they do not refund the heavy taxes, and goods imported from other provinces that are not sold in the territory are also forced to pay taxes, which is no different from Li Taxes. Only the tax rate is increased, so that merchants do not benefit from the abolition of Li Taxes, but are subject to the determination of the abolition of Li Taxes first. The Ministry of Finance should not allow the above-mentioned malpractices to occur after the abolition of Li Taxes. Our association strongly agrees and should ask your committee to return to the ministry to represent the statement that the change of the tax of this abolition is not comparable to a partial trial of a province. Each province cannot make its own atmosphere. The Ministry of Finance should strictly implement the Implementation of the Special Consumption Tax and its most important one is to strictly abide by the principle of one tax for one item and implement the refund of heavy taxes. Two, in order to facilitate the nationwide circulation after one tax, it should be collected at one time at the place of origin or concentration, and should not be collected in installments. Three, each province should not collect taxes in the name of local taxes. If the pain of the business can be eliminated in this way, the desire will be fulfilled, the business will be fortunate, and the country will be fortunate.) (18th)

Wuxi 79

Having an Affair with a Neighbor, Strangling His Wife

Lu Dabao, the son of a resident of Yantang Village, west of Nan Shuangmiao Bridge in the 15th District (Qingcheng City), is by nature wicked and prone to idleness and womanizing. In the first month of this year, he married a Miss Wang, the daughter of Wang Zhaoxiu, a migrant living nearby, through a matchmaker. After the marriage, quarrels frequently arose between the couple, and he often beat her. Recently, Dabao became infatuated with a woman surnamed Mou from a neighboring village. They became intimate, acting like husband and wife, and he viewed his wife as a thorn in his side. The other night, for some unknown reason, the couple had another argument. Dabao, in a fit of anger, took a hemp rope and strangled Miss Wang to death. Afterwards, Dabao and his father, realizing the enormity of the crime, entrusted someone to negotiate a settlement for 500 yuan as compensation for the death. They contacted Chen Tongkang and Sun Mou, relatives of the deceased in Yuqi Town, and are currently negotiating. However, local people, considering that the case involves human life and daring to settle it privately, are indignant and advocate reporting the case to the county to request an inquest and arrest the murderer to uphold justice and human dignity.

The Jiangsu Construction Department Urges the Remittance of the Canal Dredging Mu Tax

The Jiangsu Province's dredging of the Hebei Canal is of great importance. The funding for this dredging project is mainly derived from a two-cent mu tax levied on twenty-five counties in the four prefectures of Jiangbei, Huaiyang, Xuhai. The annual collection amounts to approximately 400,000 yuan, which is not a small sum. However, the county magistrates and directors of the finance bureaus often arbitrarily misappropriate or withhold funds due to local demands, so that only two or three tenths of the amount are actually remitted to the department each year. As a result, the major dredging project has not been able to proceed according to the plans made in the past. Now, during the peak season for land tax collection, a five-part reporting form has been created, modeled after the Construction Funding Management Regulations, and distributed to the county bureaus concerned for completion and submission on a旬 basis to facilitate timely assessment. No delays are allowed. This matter has been submitted to the provincial government for approval and notification to the county magistrates of the twenty-five counties in Jiangbei and Huaiyin to comply with.

Yangzhou 82

The Grand Meeting of All Circles in Jiangdu to Welcome Director Zhang

On the morning of the 20th, all circles in Jiangdu held a meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce to welcome Director Zhang and the staff of the Pacification Office. Representatives from over sixty groups, totaling more than 200 people, participated. Huang Zixian, commander of the 70th Brigade, also led his brigade's regimental commanders to participate. At 10 o'clock, the Chief of Staff and various directors of the Pacification Office arrived first, followed by Director Zhang on horseback. The entire venue welcomed him with applause. The meeting was immediately opened with a bell and music, and the rituals were performed accordingly. First, Chairman Zhang, the county magistrate, reported the purpose of the welcome, followed by a speech by Director Zhang, who stated that he did not dare to accept the welcome, but that the central government had ordered his brother to pacify Jiangsu and stationed him in Yangzhou, hoping that the elders who know the local situation in Jiangbei would instruct him. He said that during the period of political tutelage, the people are suffering from the ravages of bandits, and how can we talk about political tutelage? He also detailed the demolition of houses by people along the Pingjin Road to avoid bandits, and the daily bandit cases in Shanghai, the capital, and other places. He also discussed the Communist Party's intention to implement its doctrines, the history of Outer Mongolia's independence, the restrictions on Outer Mongolia, and the assassination of the anti-communist chairman of Outer Mongolia. Finally, he reported on the pacification plan and humbly requested guidance from all circles and understanding in all matters. Afterwards, Huang Zixian, commander of the 70th Brigade, gave a speech on the significance of the welcome. Representatives from the Chamber of Commerce, Salt Industry, and Bank then held a banquet at the Chamber of Commerce to welcome Director Zhang and the staff of the Pacification Office. The guests and hosts enjoyed themselves and dispersed.

Robbery cases have been occurring frequently in Jiangdu City. The Lugang District Security Corps received a report that a sea bandit comprador named Li Guoxiang was causing trouble in the Nankan area. He had led sea bandits to kidnap Guan Weiyi's mother from Nankan. After receiving the report, the security police were dispatched to arrest Li Guoxiang. After a preliminary trial by the Local Clearing Bureau, Li confessed to acting as a sea bandit comprador, but firmly denied the rest. It is reported that he was sent to the County Clearing Bureau for legal action on the 16th.

Nantong 84

Turning Mature Salt Fields over to the County

There are over three thousand fangli [unit of area] of old salt fields in Tongyi, accounting for two-ninths of the county's area. The fields are all mature and have long ceased to be used for boiling seawater to make salt. However, the land tax is still paid at a discounted rate, which is much lower than that of ordinary farmland, less than one-third. The county government has submitted a report to the provincial government to turn the mature salt fields over to the county, abolish idle agencies, and determine tax rates to avoid uneven burden on the people and increase tax revenue.

The Education Bureau Recovers Panji Mound

The Education Bureau has recovered Panji Mound in Nantong, which consists of 24 qing and 82 mu [unit of area]. It belonged to the Dongjian Academy during the Qing Dynasty and was used as a fund for exams. In the second year of the Republic [1913], the county council decided to use it as the county's educational property. Recently, it was discovered that the property was illegally collected by the Da Youjin Company. A special report was submitted to the Provincial Education Department, ordering the county government to recover it.

Ningbo 85

A Celebration Feast Turns into a Tragedy

He Ruilian, a resident of Chehe Pagoda in the southwestern countryside of Yin County, is 55 years old and runs a small grocery store and money exchange business. He has accumulated a small fortune, so he built a few new houses in the past few years. However, both He and his wife are old and have no children, so they adopted his nephew, Ge Changlin, as an adopted son two years ago. He is now 13 years old. However, He himself thought that his nephew was not his own son after all, so he rented a widow surnamed Ge as a temporary wife last year. As expected, she gave birth to a son. He was overjoyed and hosted a feast to invite guests, which attracted the attention of bandits. Around 12 o'clock the other night, six or seven bandits suddenly came, each holding a handgun. Two bandits first climbed over the wall and opened the main gate. The other bandits entered together. He was awakened from his sleep in the inner room and suspected it was a thief. He opened the door to look, but unexpectedly, the bandits shot him as soon as he came out. He could not dodge and was shot through the chest and died immediately. He's wife and his nephew Ge Changlin heard the commotion upstairs and came downstairs together. Ge saw what had happened to He and shouted "Uncle!" The bandits suspected that Ge was He's own son and kidnapped Ge Changlin. He's wife saw her husband die tragically and her nephew was kidnapped. She was overwhelmed with grief and wanted to die. She has reported the incident to the authorities for investigation.

Hefei 86

The Third Detachment Reduced and Reorganized into a Brigade Stationed in the Hefei, Fengtai, and Shou County Area

The General Headquarters of the Third Detachment, stationed in the Hefei, Fengtai, and Shou County area, decided to reduce and reorganize the unit into a brigade. Song Shike, the commander of the detachment, will remain the brigade commander. Yang Zhaofang was sent to Hefei as a committee member to inspect the unit. Brigade Commander Song transferred the Independent First Regiment, commanded by Cheng Zigang, stationed in Daxingji, to the Dongwai Motor Road for inspection by Committee Member Yang on the 15th. As a result of the inspection, the reorganization was carried out on the 16th. Cheng's regiment became the First Regiment of Song's Brigade, with Cheng remaining the regimental commander. Yao Haiqing became the commander of the First Battalion, Wang Shiji became the commander of the Second Battalion, Hu Renfeng, the former commander of the Fifth Regiment, became the commander of the Third Battalion, Ma Zongxian became the commander of the Artillery Company, Wang Xin became the commander of the Pistol Company, and Tao Chongxian became the commander of the Independent Company. Brigade Commander Song is scheduled to go to Fengtai by car with Committee Member Yang on the 18th to inspect the Second Regiment, commanded by Tu Shaojiu.

The Entire Town of Modian Robbed

The town of Modian, 20 li [unit of distance] northeast of here, was invaded by more than 30 bandits last night. Every household was robbed, and no one was spared. The losses were enormous.

Special Education News

Life at Wellesley College (II) 87

(Sent from the United States by Ms. Lu Erzhao of Songjiang)

(III) Student Conditions

(A) Enrollment and General Conditions

All students are female. Naturally, the United States has the most students, followed by England, then Russia and Austria. Among Asian students, the Republic of China, Japan, Korea, and the South Seas Islands are all represented. Currently, there are three Chinese students studying here, and one student each from Japan and other countries. During lectures, all students listen attentively, take notes, and their pens never stop moving. When the professor asks a question, they stand up and answer. However, the most important task is when the teacher questions them, and the most suitable task is self-study and practical experience in the library. If you only rely on a few lecture notes in the classroom, you will never have living knowledge.

During games, ball games, and swimming and other sports to exercise the body, they vigorously develop their personality. Teachers guide them and often take the lead. The students are eager to follow. Each student has a room in the dormitory, and the students take care of their own room decoration (tablecloths, curtains, etc.). The rest of the utensils are provided by the school and are fully equipped. Each room is also equipped with a wireless transmitter to prepare for the study of world-famous musicians, speakers, playwrights, and the sounds, words, and artistic aspects of songs, etc., in order to cultivate the students' temperament, morality, and virtue. American and European students are mostly members of the church and believe in Christ, with their hearts guiding their actions. The greatest result is their spirit of mutual assistance. Erzhao feels their mutual assistance everywhere, at all times, and in everything she does. Reflecting on herself, she feels deeply guilty. Is it a lack of morality? It is actually a difference in habits. This is true of the students, and even more so of the professors. Whenever there is a disaster in the world or personal hardship, they pray together and persuade people to help, doing everything they can as if they were hungry or drowning themselves. Students are young, families are like this, and schools are like this. After graduation, human society will definitely be greatly influenced.

(B) Benefits for New Students

When new students arrive at the school and are not familiar with everything, the senior students must fulfill their obligations and provide sincere guidance. This is a common practice in Western universities. Therefore, the third-year students and the first-year students are called sister classes. After entering the school, one day before the start of classes, the third-year students and the first-year students hold a meeting called the guidance meeting. Students from both grades sit in a circle on the grass, singing, talking, laughing, and discussing the past events of the school, so that the first-year students have something to follow. Thus, the new students become lively. After one or two hours, they forget each other's presence. The new students follow behind the third-year students, dancing and gesturing. The professors also join in at will, especially paying extra attention to foreign students, and sincerely guide them so that they do not suffer the hardships of a foreign country and a foreign school, based on the spirit of loving others.

(C) The Happy Day for Second-Year Students

Every year, one day within a week after the start of school is chosen as the happy day for second-year students. How happy is it? At 5 a.m. on September 23rd, the second-year students wake up the first-year students and order them to wear their clothes inside out, black socks on their feet, and flat hats on their heads. They wrap their hair, necks, and arms in green paper, making everything green (there is a saying in Western countries that first-year college students are green). After dressing up, they serve as servants in the second-year students' bedrooms, sweeping away dust carefully (every two first-year students serve one second-year student, which is an unavoidable duty). After finishing their duties, they go to class as usual after breakfast. However, on this day, wherever first-year students pass second-year students, they must pay their respects and bow to 90 degrees. The second-year students issue an order, and the first-year students obey. When entering the classroom for lessons, the first-year students must carry a pillowcase with their books placed in it, carry it on their shoulders, and hold an umbrella, as if they were Chinese monks carrying tall loads on their shoulders and carrying a musical instrument under their armpits. After 5:30 p.m., they walk slowly on the campus lawn with the group of umbrellas towering high and a mixture of music sounding, following the second-year students. The second-year students issue an order to run, and they start running. They change the order to jump, and they stop and jump. They practice the principle of obeying orders. The second-year students are like despotic monarchs of the Middle Ages. At 6:15 p.m., the monarchs resign, and the first-year and second-year students restore their classmates' spirit of friendship and love, and the class distinctions are removed. This is a common practice in the four national universities, held once a year. Erzhao thinks about it carefully. It is probably to show the glory of promotion and to warn those who stay in the same grade of the great shame. Otherwise, what is the purpose of this childish play?

(D) The Glory and Vigilance of the Graduating Class

September 21st of this year (1930) was the first Sunday after the start of school. All the students went to the chapel happily. The graduating class walked proudly in black robes and square hats. The other classes sat down first, and the music played slowly. Then, the graduating class entered in an orderly manner when the music was melodious and the entire hall was solemnly silent. Each student had a graceful bearing and a charming demeanor, like a celestial being from heaven. If a corner of a graduating student's hat was accidentally folded, the lower-class students would compete to admire it (Erzhao suddenly remembered that Guo Youdao's turban was deliberately folded when he encountered rain, and people folded the corner of their turbans in imitation. From this, we can understand the imitative nature of mankind, ancient and modern, Chinese and foreign, male and female, old and young. This heart is the same, and this principle is the same. The description of Guo Linzong's biography in the Book of Han and human emotions is extremely valuable). At that time, all eyes were focused on them. From then on, the graduating class worked hard on each course to avoid falling behind. They had a feeling of regret for the rest of their lives. If they did not graduate by this time next year and were still in the graduating class, they would have no place to put their faces. Is this also a subtle way of warning them in the award? As Mencius said, "Teaching is also multifaceted." Is this what he meant?

Important News

Inauguration of President Chu Chia-hua of National Central University 88

Government Representative Guarantees President Chu's Competence

Chu Chia-hua Takes Full Responsibility for Students' Focused Studies

At 8:00 AM on the 21st, the newly appointed President of National Central University, Chu Chia-hua, arrived at the university to assume his duties. At the same time, an oath-taking ceremony was held in the university's gymnasium. Prior to this, the university had invited representatives from various central government departments and commissions to attend the ceremony. Details of this were reported yesterday. The full details are recorded below:

On the day, attendees included Hu Hanmin, Dai Jitao, He Yingqin, Sun Wenben, Shao Yuanchong, Wang Zhongwu, Chen Yi, Ma Hetian, Chen Danian, and several dozen others. All faculty, staff, and students of the university were present. At 8:30 AM, after the ceremony was conducted with due formality, Hu Hanmin, representing the Central Party Headquarters, presided over the oath-taking. Chu Chia-hua raised his right hand and recited the oath.

Hu Hanmin's Address: Hu Hanmin delivered an address stating that today marks the inauguration of President Chu, and he felt that generally, the public thought that education in the Republic of China had progressed slowly over the past few decades, with frequent instability within schools. Some attributed this to the negative influence of the government and the disruptive activities of reactionaries and rebels everywhere. Others blamed it on the incompetence of those in charge of education and the lack of a correct direction for education. The most precious time for a person is their time in school. The late Dr. Sun Yat-sen said, "(The revolution has not yet succeeded, comrades must continue to strive for China's freedom and equality)." If a country's material civilization has progressed but its spiritual civilization remains backward, its international standing cannot be improved. When the people of a country make discoveries in academics, it indicates the level of civilization of that country. Therefore, equality in academic culture is true equality. The shame of our nation being despised by the nations of the world can only be washed away by the academic efforts of young people. The late Dr. Sun Yat-sen said, "(One must have great ambition, study diligently, and specialize to achieve great things)." University students bear a heavy responsibility for building China. Among China's 400 million people, those who are illiterate account for 80 percent. Of the remaining 20 percent, those who can receive a university education are only one in ten thousand. Therefore, students have exceptional opportunities in society, and the responsibilities they will bear in the future are greater than those of anyone else. President Chu has had success in running Sun Yat-sen University. Today, I heard a representative of Sun Yat-sen University students ask me, "Why did the central government transfer President Chu from Sun Yat-sen University to National Central University? Why is the central government so generous to Central University and so stingy to Sun Yat-sen University?" I believe that Sun Yat-sen University already has a considerable foundation and achievements, so President Chu was transferred to lead Central University. President Chu previously conducted in-depth research on natural sciences at the University of Berlin in Germany. He has also achieved success in running Sun Yat-sen University and overseeing civil affairs in Zhejiang Province. After taking over as President of National Central University, he will definitely make significant contributions in both school administration and academics. At the same time, President Chu is also a believer in the Three Principles of the People. In the future, he will educate and cultivate true talents for the construction of the Party and the country in accordance with the Three Principles of the People, making National Central University the best university in the country, which is something to be congratulated.

Dai Jitao's Address: Dai Jitao delivered an address on behalf of the National Government,

Stating that his views regarding President Chu's inauguration, based on past experience and feelings, would be simply presented to everyone. The life of a university is permanent and continuous. The oldest universities in China are only more than 30 years old (excluding those run by foreigners). National Central University is relatively young. It is hoped that National Central University will have a history of thousands of years. The lifespan of a university is the lifespan of human culture. Those who run universities should understand this point. Running a university is a permanent endeavor that should move towards the long-term future. Beautiful flowers and verdant branches are only temporary beauty and cannot be maintained permanently. Those who run universities should work diligently and not easily change their views according to temporary trends. He had been a university president for four years and was ashamed that he could not do it for life. However, he still has the responsibility to help develop Sun Yat-sen University. Those who run universities and students should consider this permanent life and not be moved by temporary beauty. Everyone should have a spirit of love, sincerity, and cooperation to create a long and bright history for Chinese universities. These were his simple opinions for everyone and President Chu.

Chen Danian's Address: Chen Danian delivered an address on behalf of the Executive Yuan, stating that the period of destruction in China has passed, and we are now in the period of political tutelage. The construction of the political tutelage period depends on the efforts of young people to explore advanced knowledge and cultivate true talents for construction. Therefore, the Executive Yuan issued an order to rectify academic style, which is for this purpose. President Chu's knowledge and morality will enable National Central University to shoulder this important mission, and so on.

Sun Wenben's Address: Sun Wenben delivered an address on behalf of the Ministry of Education, stating that National Central University has a relatively excellent position and a solid foundation among national universities, with a good academic atmosphere. It shoulders three missions for the country: (1) To promote the study of advanced knowledge and cultivate true scholars. (2) To cultivate outstanding members of society and lead society. (3) To promote Party ideology and cultivate talents for the construction of the Three Principles of the People. It is hoped that President Chu will base himself on these three major missions to create this ideal university. After Sun's speech,

Shao Yuanchong's Speech: Shao Yuanchong delivered a speech on behalf of the guests, saying that we must not be complacent and must constantly seek knowledge. Knowledge is the experience left by our predecessors. The mission of education is to use scientific methods to organize this experience so that it can be used to benefit life. Schools are places for imparting knowledge, and students should recognize and study a discipline diligently to cultivate specialized talents for construction. The progress of Chinese culture is very slow and is often looked down upon by the West, resulting in a far behind international position. In the future, to achieve international equality, we must express ourselves culturally, and the responsibility for this rests on you all. He hoped that students would bury themselves in books and do solid academic work to promote our country's inherent culture and transform world culture.

Chu Chia-hua's Reply: Finally, Chu Chia-hua delivered a reply, stating that in the future, he would sincerely accept everyone's instructions and the responsibilities entrusted to him by the government and do his job conscientiously. The president's responsibility is great, and his ability is limited, but the government's expectations for National Central University are very high, so he feels very apprehensive. National Central University bears a great responsibility for the independence of the Chinese nation and the revival of its culture. The central government wants to cultivate leaders of advanced knowledge, so it runs universities. Universities are often the center of a country's politics and culture. The late Dr. Sun Yat-sen invented the bright path of the Three Principles of the People based on science and various world knowledge. Therefore, our school should follow the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings to create true peace and a world of great harmony. From personal experience, there are uneconomical aspects in various domestic universities, resulting in a lack of learning tools. Although European and American universities have a history of several decades, they are still very economical in their use of funds and actively expand equipment and books. European and American universities often have only one lecturer in a department, and assistant teachers are also very few. In China, this is considered strange, while in foreign countries, the results are amazing. Department store-style universities in our country are very dangerous for the future of national academics and cause concern. In the future, when running this school, we should adhere to ideal standards and practical possibilities, strive to save expenses, expand equipment, and create a stable and fulfilling environment conducive to academic research. This cannot be achieved overnight or by the efforts of one person. It is hoped that everyone will work together with one heart and one mind to achieve this. National Central University was formed from the reform of Nanjing Higher Normal School and National Southeastern University. It has a history of 20 years. All the achievements in running the school and the spirit of service of graduates in society have been heard to some extent. Unfortunately, there has been instability in the school recently, which is very regrettable. You will soon leave school and serve in society. The precious time for studying is very short. It is hoped that you will cherish the time you spend at school and no longer be distracted by external affairs, causing factional disputes within the school. The progress of the school is to provide a stable environment for you to study in peace. He has a responsibility for the educational policy and school administration. How to enable you to acquire advanced knowledge so that you can strive for society in the future is even clearer and more practical than your parents. In the future, he will do his best to assist you in achieving the ultimate goal of university. At the beginning of his taking office, he was not yet clear about the internal affairs of the school, and a concrete plan for improving school affairs could not be discussed for the time being. The above is just a temporary feeling. After the speech, the meeting was adjourned.

Hangzhou's Plan for Universal Compulsory Education 90

To ensure that all children in the city receive education in eight years.

The Hangzhou Municipal Government, in view of the large number of out-of-school children in Hangzhou, as revealed by a recent survey of over 20,000, this phenomenon is due to the urban social recession, and also due to insufficient education funding. Therefore, a plan has been specially formulated to increase education funding year by year over eight years to ensure that all children in the city receive compulsory education. According to the plan, the total education funding for the 20th year of the Republic is 424,640 yuan, with 27,406 children in school and 20,000 children out of school. From the 21st year of the Republic, education funding will be increased by 70,000 yuan each year, reducing the number of out-of-school children by 3,000. By the 27th year of the Republic, the total education budget will be 883,840 yuan, with 48,000 children in school and no children out of school.

The Provincial Department of Education Orders Yangzhou Middle School Not to Exceed the Budget for Construction 92

The Department of Education previously received a request from Yangzhou Middle School to use the surplus of 17,000 yuan from the accommodation fees of the 17th and 18th years of the Republic to build an auditorium and a science hall. This was approved, and the school was ordered to submit a detailed budget for review. However, several months passed without the plan being submitted. Yesterday, it was reported that the bids received exceeded the budget by more than double. The Department of Education believes that the school did not follow the original plan, and since the provincial education funds for the 19th year of the Republic are very tight, it is impossible to allocate additional funds to cover the construction shortfall. It has already instructed the school to follow the previous order and find ways to reduce the project within the existing budget. The original order is recorded below:

The submission and attachments have been reviewed. Previously, the school president requested to use the surplus of accommodation fees from the 17th and 18th years of the Republic and the temporary fees from the 18th year of the Republic to build an auditorium, classrooms, and laboratories, stating that the estimated price was close to the total amount of the surplus. The Department approved the use of the 17,000 yuan surplus as the total amount of the school's temporary fees for the 19th year of the Republic and ordered that a comprehensive plan be made within this range for all necessary construction and equipment and submitted for approval and implementation. However, the school president did not comply with the order to submit the plan for review and instead invited merchants to bid. It is now reported that the bids received exceeded the original budget by more than 20,000 yuan, which is clearly inconsistent with the original plan. As for the temporary fees for the 19th year of the Republic, the 22nd meeting of the Education Funding Committee decided that temporary fees should be temporarily postponed until the provincial education funds are insufficient to pay regular expenses. Therefore, the request to allocate temporary fees for the 19th year of the Republic will be temporarily set aside by the Department. The school is still required to follow the previous order and find ways to reduce the project within the existing budget and report the handling situation for record. The attachments will be temporarily stored here.

Gu Zhongyi's New Contribution to School Dramas 96

Mr. Gu Zhongyi, currently a professor in the Department of Foreign Languages at National Jinan University, has written extensively. Recently, in view of the lack of school dramas, he specially compiled and translated 50 dramas, divided into ten collections, specifically for use in dramas at all levels of schools and in small theaters. The first collection, "Uncle Liu San," and the second collection, "The Face Worth One Hundred and Twenty-Five Taels of Silver," have already been printed, and the remaining eight collections are being prepared.

Mr. Gu has translated many works. Published works include "The Merchant of Venice" (New Moon Publishing), "Meroe's Scent" (Kaiming, now re-issued), "The Rat Has Skin" (Commercial Press), "Sisters" and "Flowers in Paradise" and "Small Satires of Life" (all from Zhenmei Shan), "Selections of English and American One-Act Plays," and "Selections of English and American Speeches" (Beixin). Recently, Kaiming published a selection of Hardy short stories, including "The Three Strangers," "The Missed Marriage," and "The Adored One," all of which are Hardy's most famous novels. Coupled with Mr. Gu's lively writing style and expressive translation, those who love literature should not miss it.

Northeast Basketball Team 100

Arrives in Shanghai on January 17th

The Northeast University basketball team, which won the Shenyang City Championship, is quite strong. It plans to take advantage of the winter vacation to go south and practice and compete with famous teams in Shanghai. The Sports Association received a letter from the school yesterday requesting assistance in arranging competitions. The team, led by Song Junfu, is expected to arrive in Shanghai around January 17th and plans to stay at Jiaotong University in Xujiahui.

Municipal No. 1 Field Small Football Tournament, Yiming Bing Wins the Jian'er Group Championship 103

Although it was drizzling yesterday, the Municipal No. 1 Public Sports Field Small Football Tournament continued as scheduled. The results are recorded below:

Group Match Result

Youth Yule vs. Guan B Both teams forfeited

Youth Yiming Wins Youning 7-3

Youth Zhong B Wins Shangchu 1-0

Jian'er Huguang Wins Black Eagle 1-0

Jian'er Zhong Bing Wins Chenguang 1-0

Jian'er Yiming Nei Wins Shi Bing 5-3

Jian'er Chaowei Wins Shangwen 1-0

Jian'er Guantong Wins Tonghui 1-0

Among the matches, the battle between Yiming Bing and Shi Bing was the most moving. Yiming Bing had been invincible, and Shi Bing had been unstoppable. Only last week, the score was tied with Zhong Bing. Yesterday was the final match, and the championship would be decided in this one game. On the battlefield, Yiming Bing immediately launched an attack. Center Yue Renli fought alone, breaking through the camp and successfully scoring the first goal, which won applause from the audience. Continuing the melee, Shi Bing's momentum gradually increased, and their midfielder also scored a goal, tying the score. In the second half, Yiming Bing knew that the enemy could not be underestimated, and the three forwards launched a full-scale attack. Left forward Ding Bingkun received the support of the center and flipped over to score a goal. Yue Renxiao followed up with another goal, greatly boosting morale. Shi Bing desperately counterattacked and also scored two goals, again tying the score. Yiming Bing was deeply afraid of losing the victory, so they desperately advanced, and Yue Renxiao showed his power again, using his nimble and lively skills and experience on the battlefield to strike hard again, scoring two goals, thus winning the Jian'er group championship with a score of five to three. In general, although Shi Bing's talent was very organized, the connection between the front and rear lines, the agility of the movements, and the accuracy of the shots were far inferior to Yiming Bing's. The winning of the championship was not accidental.
