Free Talk

A Record of Japanese Go Master Honinbo Shusai and His 162

Pudong Disciple Jue Mi

Mr. Tao Shen'an Hongxiang from Lujiahang, Pudong, is one of the disciples of the Japanese Go master Honinbo Shusai. In Japan, Go players of the 3rd or 4th dan are called high-level players, those of the 5th, 6th, or 7th dan are called masters, those of the 8th dan are called quasi-masters, and those of the 9th dan are called masters. Honinbo Shusai is a 9th dan master. Currently, there is only one 9th dan master in Japan, and that is Honinbo Shusai. Tao had no teacher in Go at first. Because of his love for it, he devoted himself to this art. From a young age, he studied the Go scores of his predecessors and was familiar with the Go scores of all dynasties in our country. Therefore, in a few years, his Go skills greatly improved and he had no equal in his hometown. He read the Go scores of famous Japanese players and admired Honinbo Shusai, so he treated him as a disciple and asked him for advice. Honinbo Shusai, seeing that his Go skills were extraordinary, also accepted him as a disciple, gave him guidance, and exchanged letters with him every day. His skills greatly improved. At the same time, Zhang Danru and Wang Ziyan were also remotely learning from Honinbo Shusai. Zhang was a famous figure in Shanghai who loved Go all his life and was rich in wealth. He always tried to recruit anyone in the country who was skilled in this art. Therefore, his guests were often full, mostly famous figures in the country. Hearing of Tao's reputation, he recruited Tao and treated him as an honored guest. Wang Ziyan was Zhang's tutor and taught at Zhang's house. From then on, the three of them were known as close friends. Tao's family was a prominent family in Lujiahang, and because he inherited the legacy of his ancestors, he was well-fed and well-clothed. Moreover, he was quiet and indifferent and lived in the countryside all his life, not asking about worldly affairs or seeking fame. He only devoted himself to Go. My sister's husband, Mr. Zhu Futian, was from the same village as him. In the Jiazi year, to celebrate the 100th birthday of his father and son, he founded the Jiazi Primary School in Xinlu Town as a memorial to the 100th birthday of his father and son. Because Tao was too idle, he was hired as the principal. Tao also took it upon himself. In his spare time, Tao taught students about seasonal flowers or taught teachers about Go. Therefore, at that time, many teachers at Jiazi were able to play Go and many students were able to garden. Duan Qirui loved Go all his life. When he was in power, he heard of Tao's reputation and sent a special envoy to the south to invite Tao to the capital. Tao's mother and wife both wanted him to go to the capital and prepared luggage and clothes for him, costing hundreds of yuan. But Tao was reluctant to go. Not long after, Duan stepped down and Tao did not go to the capital. In the autumn of the following year, he died of dysentery at the age of only thirty-odd. Before his death, he wrote a book called "Essence of Japanese Go", which collected the Go games of various Japanese Go players, extracted the essence and used it broadly, translated it into Chinese, and added commentary. Therefore, it was called "Essence". The manuscript had just been completed and had not been collated when Tao died. After Tao's death, Wang Ziyan found the book when mourning Tao and collated it for him. Zhang Danru asked someone to write a preface for it and had it published in the world. The book was printed in Japan, and the version was exquisite and cost over a thousand yuan. If Tao knew in the afterlife that he had obtained this confidant after his death, he would have no regrets. During his lifetime, the Japanese Go Institute had approached him with a dan rank, but it is not known which dan it was, either 4th dan or 5th dan, but it was probably between 4th and 5th dan, and he was undoubtedly a first-class figure in our country's Go. It is a pity that our country had such talent in Go but died so early. What a pity!

A Laughing Matter Haike 163

Man (presenting a large bouquet of roses to his girlfriend): Miss C, I heard that today is your twentieth birthday. I have nothing to celebrate with. I know that you love roses the most, so I offer this bouquet to express my sincere wishes.

Woman (extraordinarily happy, smelling the flowers again and again): Thank you, you can please me so much that I am extremely happy (uncontrollably kissed the man)

Man (flattered): Miss C, I...

Woman (blushing): I'm sorry, I offended you

Man: No, no, I'm going to buy another bouquet of roses, can you still give me a kiss like this?

Fat country woman (going to Da Gong to buy things, taking the elevator, saying to the driver): Go up, go up

Driver: What floor?

Fat country woman: I want to buy furniture, which floor is it on?

Driver: That's on the fifth floor.

Fat country woman (looking at the small driver): I see that you are such a small person, but you have the strength to take me up?

Woman: Dear, you just keep saying that you love me, love me, I don't know if you really love me in your heart?

Man: I really love you wholeheartedly.

Woman: What proof do you have?

Man: Last night, when I said goodbye to you and kissed you, your dog bit a piece of meat from my leg, but I didn't even feel it, so you can know that I am focused on you.

Research on the Drama Lyrics of Mei Lanfang's Farewell My Concubine 164

Mei Huaguanzhu

The drama "Farewell My Concubine" occupies a very important position in the old dramas. Every time Mei Wan Hua comes to the south, the ticket sales for the night of "Farewell My Concubine" will increase several times. Its magic is truly extraordinary. I have seen this drama three times. The first time was at the Tianchan Stage, when Xiaolou played Xiang Yu, which was of course very wonderful. The second time was at the Gong Stage, because Xiaolou did not come with him, the role of Overlord had to be played by Zhou Rui'an. The appearance was similar, but the spirit was not, and the difference was far away. The third time was at the Daxin Stage (now the Tianchan Stage). The Overlord was Jin Shaoshan. Although Shaoshan did not have Xiaolou's solemnity and composure, his dark and wailing singing voice was enough to give the audience considerable satisfaction. This time when I came to the south, this drama was performed once. I was too busy to go and watch it, but according to my friends, Shaoshan's skills have been deepening recently, and the fire has disappeared. Compared with a few years ago, he is much more brilliant. Although Hua's age has increased, because of his wonderful makeup, his appearance has not decreased. As for his performance and expressions, of course, he has been improving with the times and becoming more and more vivid.

Wan Hua灌(recorded) by Bei Kai Company (Since I followed the King to conquer the east and fight the west, I have suffered from wind, frost and toil year after year. I only hate that the merciless Qin smeared the creatures with charcoal, which aroused the heroes to chase the deer in the Central Plains) The four sentences of the original singing of the slow board, melting the new tune and the old tune in one furnace, have a different kind of realm. No one else can sing this well. In the autumn of this year, a certain gentleman in the Liyuan Public Report doubted Wan Hua's slow board of Farewell My Concubine, saying that Wan Hua had always sang the shaken board on the stage (since I··) in the four sentences, but now in the Bei Kai movie, he suddenly changed to singing the slow board, thinking that it was necessary to study it, and said that the rules of the play fundamentally cannot change the shaken board to the slow board. I didn't dare to believe Mr. so-and-so's theory at the time, because I knew very well that Wan Hua did sing the slow board once at the Gong Stage, not the shaken board (there is a record in my previous work "Little Shenbao" at that time). However, I didn't want to be too confident, so I wrote to Wan Hua himself, asking him to answer truthfully to clear up the doubts. In a few days, Wan Hua sent me a reply saying (since I followed the King··) The four sentences of the original singing of the slow board were later changed to the shaken board because the time of the whole play was sometimes too long, but it was not inevitable. When recording the film, it was based on the original singing method, so it was a slow board. Singing the shaken board on the stage is indeed a temporary way to change it, as Mr. So-and-so said). According to this, we can know that singing the slow board is the right way, and singing the shaken board is not suitable.

A certain celebrity in Beiping has a little talent and usually pretends to be clever and likes to tamper with the lyrics of famous actors for fun. I once remembered that this gentleman also擅added删改changed for the slow board of 別姫Farewell My Concubine (since I···), changing the third and fourth sentences (恨祇恨無道秦把生靈塗炭才惹得衆豪傑逐鹿中原Hate only hate the merciless Qin smeared the creatures with charcoal, which aroused the heroes to chase the deer in the Central Plains) to (何日裏方得免兵戈擾亂消却了衆百姓困苦哀憐What day will we be able to avoid the chaos of war and eliminate the suffering and pity of the people). I don't think the original lyrics are 落落大方generous and natural, which is exactly the tone of Yu Ji. The gentleman's changed sentences are not only not grand, but also the sentence structure is not as飄逸有致 elegant as the original lyrics.點金成鐵 Turning gold into iron is self-defeating. Those like the gentleman can be said to be ignorant of self-measurement.

Travels in Southeast Asia (107) 165

It is difficult to judge whether jade is good or bad when it is in the rough stone, and even experts cannot be sure. Looking at the gray stone surface, cutting it open may be worth millions or worthless, which shows how difficult it is to know the rough stone. In the past, Bian He obtained a rough stone in Jing Mountain and knew that it was a priceless treasure, but the king did not believe it and listened to slander and had his feet cut off. Bian He wept while holding the rough stone, and later it was found to be a wall of Liancheng. But it is very difficult for those who know it at the beginning. Those who work in this industry may spend millions of gold without any gains, or they may get fish by raising a net. One person worked in this industry for decades without any gains, but once he got a treasure worth hundreds of thousands, which is like the inventor's six hundred and sixth time.

On the 16th, the KMT branch welcomed and gave a speech on the success of the domestic revolution and the beginning of the world revolution. On the 17th, I went to the Dongmiu area for a gathering. The gathering lasted for several days. Many women were seen in the city. The things sold in the market were simple and crude, like the village gatherings in our small villages. However, there were many clay Buddha statues, and the custom of men and women dancing in front of the gods was prevalent, with young people being the majority and occasional elderly people with white hair. The music and dance were also rhythmic. Traveling two or three miles southwest from Dongmiu, a small boat can reach a winding creek. There is also a large gathering place where men and women dance in front of the gods, but they do not take off their shoes and are not allowed to go ashore. The boatman guided us to bypass the bank to avoid the trouble of taking off our shoes. The boats coming and going greeted each other, and the men and women joked and sang and danced crazily. I do not understand the language, but people say that during these days, the men and women who come to the meeting are all for the purpose of liberating marriage, making an appointment to come, and taking advantage of the gathering to be a period of free marriage, so the boys have no scruples and mostly say words of love to the women. According to this, it is the same as Plato's ideal state of God. How can religion hinder free love? It is even carried out in the name of God. During this meeting, the Chinese also participated, and stayed in the Chinese Guanyin Temple to gamble for several days, because there was nothing else to do. Gambling is not only the case for capital merchants, but also for workers, and even newspaper staff are inevitably involved in gambling. The gambling style in Southeast Asia is like this, and it is difficult for the nation to have hope for progress.

There is a major shortcoming in the "Farewell My Concubine" drama that others do not pay much attention to. Only the host of 婝, 婝主人 (the host is Prince Xun of the Qing Dynasty, and 婝is his other name. He has a deep understanding of 皮黃, and has a unique insight to see the flaws), who has a deep research on 皮黃(Beijing opera), pointed out the flaws and said that the words念(recited) by Yu Ji (可憐無定河邊骨猶是春閨夢裏人Pitiful are the bones by the boundless river, still dreaming of home in their spring boudoirs) are Tang Dynasty poems. Yu Ji was born before the Tang Dynasty, and it is inappropriate to quote Tang Dynasty poems in the drama. The host once had revised words, and I have also seen them, but I cannot remember them because I am forgetful.

A New Deceptive Technique Using Counterfeit Currency 166

The methods of defrauding landlords in Shanghai are constantly emerging, as this column has repeatedly reported. However, none are as unique, creative, and remarkably strange as what a relative of mine encountered. I am writing about it and submitting it to this column to reveal its secrets, so that those in Shanghai who have vacant houses for rent can be vigilant.

My relative, Mr. Yi, rents a house in a lane on Avenue Edward VII in West Shanghai. The house has two floors above ground. Mr. Yi doesn't have a large family, so he rents out the remaining rooms. Recently, the tenant of the three rooms above the parlor moved out. Mr. Yi posted a rental advertisement at the entrance of the lane to attract tenants. Within two short hours, a couple appeared, claiming to be looking for a place to live. It was already 3 PM when they arrived. Mr. Yi was out on business, so Mrs. Yi, as usual, led them upstairs to inspect the rooms. The couple's clothing was very fashionable, and their speech was refined, resembling that of the upper class. After the inspection, they seemed quite satisfied. After inquiring about the rent and slightly negotiating it down, they agreed on the price and said they would move in the next day. Mrs. Yi then asked for a deposit of two silver dollars, as it is customary in Shanghai to pay a deposit after agreeing to rent a house to avoid misunderstandings. Upon hearing this, the gentleman took out a wallet filled with banknotes. After examining them for a long time, he smiled and said to Mrs. Yi, "I left home in a hurry today, and all I have is ten-dollar bills. I wonder if you can find eight dollars in change?" Hearing this, Mrs. Yi reached into her pocket, took out her wallet, and saw that she only had six dollars. She then turned to the maid and asked her to take the gentleman's ten-dollar bill to the tobacco shop to exchange it. The gentleman said, "That won't be necessary. Please return the banknote to me, and I will exchange it myself and pay the deposit later." He seemed to distrust Mr. Yi's maid. Mrs. Yi understood and, fearing that the gentleman would not return, borrowed two silver dollars from a housemate to make up the eight dollars and gave it to the gentleman. The gentleman briefly checked it and put it in his pocket, instructing her to clean the rented rooms so he could move in the next day. After saying this, he bid farewell and left. Mrs. Yi then ordered the maid to take the banknote paid by the gentleman to exchange it, but the maid returned and said that the banknote was a fake and worthless. Only then did Mrs. Yi realize she had been deceived. When Mr. Yi returned, she told him what had happened. Mr. Yi couldn't help but be speechless and deeply admired the fraudster's cleverness and meticulous planning.

Warmth in My Heart (340) by Bao Tianxiao 167

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Earnestly Seeks Instruction from a Teacher, a Heroine Generously Discusses Military Affairs at a Brothel.

Zuo Shichen said, "It's not like that. People like you don't need to pursue profound knowledge when you study. Being able to recognize a few more characters and understand the meaning of texts is good enough, and gaining a little more knowledge is convenient for yourself. If you want to study, there is a girls' school on Threemile Road that has established a special class specifically for women who have lost the opportunity to study since childhood. It doesn't limit age or ask about family background. You can sign up and choose a subject, and it's only an hour or two each day. Anyway, you get up early and only have things to do after the lights are lit. With your intelligence, you'll definitely learn something."

Lü Yi shook her head and said, "I won't go. If I weren't in a brothel, studying would be open and aboveboard. Now, going to school during the day as a female student, but running around at night and performing in a brothel, it's like studying is also secretive. Of course, I can't tell people at school that I'm a prostitute, but if the classmates find out, even if they don't attack me, the whispers behind my back would be unbearable. If the headmaster of the school knows that I'm a prostitute and kicks me out, where would I put my face? Wouldn't that be seeking honor but incurring humiliation instead? A Suo also has a younger sister there studying. She's quite smart. When it's time for class, she grabs her book bag and goes to school. After class, she goes straight home and doesn't dare to dress up at all, keeping a plain face. She doesn't even dare to wear silk clothes, only wearing a patriotic cloth qipao. But later, her classmates found out. The teachers didn't say anything, but the classmates' cold words were really unbearable. She cried a lot afterwards and refused to go anymore."

Zuo Shichen said, "In principle, education doesn't distinguish between noble and lowly, and doesn't ask about social class. Confucius said, 'Education should be provided to all, without discrimination,' which means that everyone should receive education, regardless of their background. So why can't prostitutes receive education? However, they think that prostitutes are always of questionable character and always romantic, and they are afraid that one or two people might corrupt others, so they have to guard against that. Therefore, it's okay if the school authorities don't know, but if they do find out, it's indeed a bit difficult."

At this moment, Lü Yi's mother interjected, "Originally, I also told her to go to Threemile Road to study, but she said the same thing. Actually, she really wakes up at ten in the morning. After eating, she sits around doing nothing. There's really nothing to do, so she just plays mahjong. Second Master, why don't you come and teach her a little bit every day? That way, she can recognize more characters and relieve her loneliness."

Zuo Shichen said, "Oh, teach me to be a teacher? I'm very strict! If you can't read, I'll spank you!"

Lü Yi said, "If you're really willing to come and teach, you can spank me if I can't read! But a teacher has to have a teacher's demeanor! Well then, starting tomorrow, you'll come and teach me for one hour every day."

Commercial News

Turbulent Gold Market Last Week 168

The surge in the gold market last week was even more intense than the previous week, breaking previous records. However, the situation from the beginning of the week, when the price of silver futures plummeted by ten taels, was the opposite of before. This time, the bears covered their positions, adding three or four taels. The reason for this was that the end of the Gregorian calendar year was approaching, and there was a lack of cash. The bulls did not dare to absorb the losses and instead changed to posting losses. The market suddenly soared, progressing rapidly. This was because overseas markets continued to fall sharply, and large silver bars suddenly broke through fifteen points. In the statistics for this week, the price fell by 4.375. The price of American silver also dropped to 0.625, so the Shanghai exchange rate became tight. However, there were constant fluctuations, and the exchange rate for Changtong silver only increased by half a point (0.125). The daily exchange rate only rose by 0.0125. However, none of these were as sharp as the gold market. The gold rush was unusually turbulent, and the huge waves could not be suppressed. Every day, there were fluctuations of more than ten taels, changing rapidly and unpredictably. Industry insiders were at a loss. In short, the news was mixed. There was an atmosphere of economic depression and a silver market crash in the United States. However, this did not materialize. Moreover, there were sometimes reports of silver being produced. As a result, people were hesitant. On Thursday, a Reuters report announced that the United States was unable to save the silver shortage at the London International Conference, and it was also heard that Russia had suddenly closed Japanese banks (fearing that the Japanese-American exchange rate would rise). The market received this news, which was enough to arouse the interest of general speculators. Major players such as Mr. Wu and Mr. Luo began to scramble to buy, and the bears were forced to cover their positions due to the environment. The market soared, suddenly breaking through the sixty-tael mark. However, many of the previous bulls took advantage of this opportunity to sell and make a profit. Then, rumors suddenly spread that Chase Bank would ship a large amount of cash abroad. The news spread, and the market suddenly saw a new era of 671 taels, unprecedented in history. The surge finally subsided at the end of the week. The silver market and exchange rate seemed to stabilize slightly. As a result, the price increased by 61 taels and 4 mace, an increase of about 20 taels compared to the previous Saturday (excluding the 3 taels for futures). Compared to the opening price on the first day of the swap, the increase was 23 taels and 9 mace. The difference between the highest and lowest prices for February was 37 and a half taels, which was also a large amount. According to the daily exchange rate, the price was actually 30 taels lower. Otherwise, it would have reached a peak of 700 taels. However, it is said that the future path is limited. The bid price only increased by five or six taels. The general situation of the week is described in detail below.

The price rose by more than two taels. From Monday, the exchange rate for large silver bars rose by 0.125, the price of silver rose by 0.25, and the exchange rate listing did not change. The domestic market was tight and then eased. As for the gold market in the current month, the price changed from sharp to soft. In the morning, it had reached 49 and a half taels. In the afternoon, because the swap was opened early privately, the price was slightly suppressed. The market closed at 31 taels and 1 mace at the 30-tael mark, a sharp drop of 9 taels and 9 mace compared to the previous Saturday. On this day, the major player Mr. Lu of Shangyu Dahe sold heavily through Hengxingyuan and Xie. Xinhang also sold some. The next day, the price suddenly turned high due to the swap. Bond Market Quiet This Past Week 171

The bond market in Shanghai has been more quiet this past week, with trading being unusually slow. This quietness has not been seen for a long time. This is because the end of the year is approaching, and all industries are engaged in winding up their affairs, and the bond market environment has not changed at all. Major traders are watching and not moving. Excluding the first day of the week, when nearly 9 million was traded, and Tuesday and Thursday, when over 6 million was traded, the average daily trading volume was only about 4 million. The total trading volume for the week was 34.205 million, a decrease of over 9.5 million compared to the previous week. The 19th Customs bonds were still active, accounting for 10.47 million, with 4.56 million for December and 5.91 million for January. Other bonds, such as the demobilization bonds, accounted for 3.7 million for December and 3.485 million for January; the reorganization treasury bonds accounted for 2.815 million for December and 2.515 million for January; the 19th rehabilitation bonds accounted for 2.79 million for December and 2.15 million for January; the 96th public bonds accounted for 1.38 million for December and 2.055 million for January; the 6% bonds accounted for 455,000 for December and 640,000 for January; the customs duties accounted for 600,500 for December and 415,000 for January. Other bonds were even more scarce. The 19th cigarette bonds accounted for only 515,000, the financial bonds accounted for 115,000, the rehabilitation bonds accounted for 90,000, the 7-year bonds accounted for 10,000, and there were no transactions for the subsequent 25 and accumulated cigarette bonds. The spot market was also extremely quiet, with a total trading volume of 79,500 for the week, with the 19th customs bonds accounting for 40,600 and the demobilization bonds accounting for 14,000. Other bonds accounted for only a few thousand. The price changes of the bonds were minimal due to the stable situation and the unchanged bond market environment. As the end of the Gregorian year approached, all industries were engaged in winding up their affairs, so there was little trading activity, and the trend became even more sluggish. The daily fluctuations were very small, with the largest fluctuations for each bond being only a few angles per yuan. The financial, 96th, rehabilitation, and customs bonds fluctuated by only about half a yuan. The results, compared to the previous week, were mixed, with gains and losses offsetting each other. The 6% bonds rose by about 1 yuan, while the demobilization and current-term mobilization bonds each rose by over 1 yuan. The market situation is difficult to improve in the short term. Cotton Yarn Auction Ends Well This Past Week 172

However, Current Consumer Spending is Extremely Weak

The initial trend of the Shanghai cotton yarn market was unpredictable this past week, with the exception of a good two tael in auctions. Due to the weakening global situation and the approaching end of the year, actual sales were sluggish, and Chaozhou merchants and Japanese traders unanimously dumped their holdings, causing the market to reach a new low price. Shortly after, American cotton slightly improved, and the matter of export duties greatly boosted the market. Factories in the interior, as a precaution, purchased more than 1,000 bales of yarn, greatly shocking the market and tightening prices. However, actual sales were particularly quiet throughout the week. The lowest price for the current month's yarn was 135 taels and 5 mace, and the highest price was 140 taels and 0 mace and 3 mace. As a result, the price of each month was up to two taels higher than the previous week.

The cotton market has been relatively healthy, and the cotton market is still firm. Due to the strange changes in the exchange rate, the supply from various sources is not smooth, resulting in a limited amount of base goods, and the bulls have been very strong, refusing to loosen their grip in the near term. However, the cotton markets in the United States and India are extremely weak, so Chinese and foreign factories have switched to purchasing foreign cotton because of its lower price. Chinese cotton has been completely eroded by foreign cotton, and many traders have been dumping their holdings, indicating that the struggle between the bulls and bears is fierce. At the end of the week, the American cotton government announced that it would continue to maintain cotton prices, which boosted people's confidence and increased the market price. The cotton market is currently unpredictable, with fluctuations of about one or two taels. The price of each month's cotton in the auction was up six or seven mace compared to the previous week.

Grain and Rice Market Continues to Stabilize 175

Yesterday, the various gangs in Zhabei saw about 30 rice boats sailing north, and sales were very smooth. Sales of high-quality goods were particularly strong, with prices particularly high, opening at 14 yuan. Although there was no change in the secondary market, the situation was clearly stable and secretly loose. This was because both the shops and customers were watching, and the buying interest had eased. The supply of thin rice was scarce at the source, with only a few inquiries from the countryside. The market situation was unchanged. The top-quality Yangxian rice was in short supply, and the market price was high, with eager customers. The price was between 12.96 and 7 jiao. The sales of Duxian and Buxian rice were sluggish, and the price remained stable. Sales were not smooth, and the price of Yinyuan rice was also flat. The market was generally flat.

Yesterday, about 10 boats arrived at the south of Shanghai. The common gang machine japonica rice market had shifted to a volatile situation. Sales of high-quality goods were brisk, while sales of secondary goods were not strong. The price of Su Tong white japonica rice also rose, and the price of secondary goods was suppressed. The market price was stable, but there were small fluctuations of around an angle. The price of top-quality Su Gang rice gradually reached around 13 yuan. Early-season and early rice in the South Gang were slightly tight due to the arrival of dry rice and reports of firmness from the production areas, but the overall trend was not good. Sales of Yangdu and other indica rice were sluggish, and the arrival price was close to the exchange rate. There were very few buyers of Yinyuan rice, and the special goods were still depressed, so the market price was slightly soft.

Silk and Tea: Static Silk Market This Past Week 176

Foreign Silk Merchants are Unmoving

Overseas Silk Telegrams are Not Transferring, and There is Transaction But No Market for European and American Chinese Silk

Cloth Factories' Appetite is Not Smooth, Shanghai Silk Factories Have Ceased Production Early

The Shanghai Foreign Merchant Silk Market has been even more silent this past week due to the increasingly precarious economies of overseas nations. Bankruptcies are reported daily, and most silk weaving factories have ceased production. The consumption of raw silk has decreased, and the stocks are piling up. There has been no movement in factory sales, and New York and Lyon have not had a market for raw silk for two weeks. Telegraphs from Shanghai have been similarly unresponsive. The 30-odd silk factories that are still running have been trying to clear their stocks of silk by the end of the year, but the stocks are increasing rapidly. The financial situation at the end of the year is increasingly tight, and silk cocoon loan repayments are being urged. With silk but no place to borrow against it, and no funds for capital turnover, the silk factories are ceasing operations early for the New Year holiday in order to save on expenses. Since the beginning of this past week, another 20 or so silk factories have continued to cease operations. In the middle of the past week, domestic cloth merchants made some purchases, and Indian merchants covered some short positions, trading dozens of packages of yellow and white silk. The silk price has continued to weaken, and Chinese merchants are suffering losses, while foreign merchants are stagnating. There is transaction but no market for Chinese silk overseas. The raw silk market has not been extensively reported.
